### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?

## Section 008: Verification Gate Command Set
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?

- **supporting_reason:** Section 008 "Verification Gate Command Set", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because a memory system's verification is bidirectional, entries are checked at write time for resumability and snapshots are checked at read time against reality, the two gates bracketing the storage they protect

## Section 021: Retry Backpressure Guidance
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed corpus-process bullets stand beside what the family implies for practice failures, a journal found unresumable at resume time is repaired forward, a fresh evidence-based checkpoint reconstructed from repository state, never backfilled into history, a script failure downgrades practice to the manual template with review compensation until tooling returns, and repeated unresumable journals from one workstream signal grain problems, entries too coarse, addressed by cadence and grain, not by abandoning the contract
- **supporting_reason:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the family's append-only law shapes all repair, corrections are new entries, so every failure response reduces to write forward honestly, the ledger discipline applied to its own breakdowns
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: the erosion path is quiet abandonment, a workstream whose journal failed once at resume concluding the practice does not work and reverting to memory, the exact failure mode the family exists to prevent, now unrecorded

## Section 022: Observability Checklist

- **supporting_reason:** Section 022 "Observability Checklist", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the contract is an observability schema in disguise, its sections are exactly the state variables of a development session, and fixing them across all checkpoints makes session state queryable over time like any well-schemaed telemetry
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 022 "Observability Checklist", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: free-form journaling destroys queryability even when content is complete, the same information scattered across prose cannot answer which checkpoints were in Red or which tests stayed failing longest without a human rereading everything

## Section 023: Performance Verification Method
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed latency packet stands beside the family's performance surface, the contract reserves a permanent performance-and-metrics section in every frame, the workflow lists performance regression discovery among checkpoint triggers, and the persona's guideline records benchmarks established during development, together treating performance numbers as session state to preserve, not gates to enforce

- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: leaving the metrics section perpetually empty on performance-relevant work silently deletes the baseline history a future regression investigation will need

## Section 024: Scale Boundary Statement
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed task-splitting bounds stand beside the family's own scale limits, one journal per feature or ticket by the workflow's first rule, frames bounded by the seven-section contract, workstreams scaled by adding journals rather than growing them, and the family's authority ending at session-state management, it tracks TDD work and never directs what to build or how to test
- **supporting_reason:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the one-journal-per-workstream rule keeps each file's state space coherent, mixing features in one journal makes phase and next-steps ambiguous, the sections assume a single workstream's answers
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: the monolithic journal is the characteristic scale failure, one file absorbing an entire project until its current phase means nothing and resumers must read all history to find their thread
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: scale limits of the practice, this evolution's own task splitting keeps the seed paragraphs
- **revision_decision:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to state the three boundaries, journal per workstream, frame per contract, and state-management-only authority
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that this corpus scaled the family's design to four parallel lanes plus a master journal, per-lane journals for workstream state and a master for corpus-level state, a two-tier extension the entrypoints never describe but their per-workstream rule implies, the local deployment discovering the composition rule the doctrine left implicit
